PROCEDURE buka_barang
THISFORM.CEk_limit
XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,XS1+XS2+XS3+xs4+xs5+XS6+XS7+XS8+XS9+" "+XLIMIT,"BRG")
IF xh<>1 
   MESSAGEBOX("Database gagal diakses 1!!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   RETURN
ENDI 
ENDPROC
PROCEDURE cek_limit
nMax_Row=thisform.pageframe1.page1.xPerPage.Value
nMaxPage = INT((nTotRec + nMAX_ROW - 1) / nMAX_ROW)
thisform.pageframe1.page1.xmaxPage.Value=nMaxPage
xCurrentPage=thisform.pageframe1.page1.xCurrentPage.Value
nCurrentPage = MIN(MAX(xCurrentPage, 1), nMaxPage + 1)
thisform.pageframe1.page1.xCurrentPage.Value=nCurrentPage
nFirstRow = (nCurrentPage - 1) * nMAX_ROW
IF (nFirstRow + nMAX_ROW) < nTotRec
   nRowCount = nMAX_ROW
ELSE
   nRowCount = MAX(nTotRec - nFirstRow, 0)
ENDIF
IF thisform.pageframe1.page1.xcurrentPage.Value=thisform.pageframe1.page1.xmaxPage.Value
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xmajuPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xAkhirPage.Enabled=.f.
else   
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xmajuPage.Enabled=.t.
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xAkhirPage.Enabled=.t.
endi   
IF thisform.pageframe1.page1.xcurrentPage.Value=1
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xmundurPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xAwalPage.Enabled=.f.
ELSE
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xmundurPage.Enabled=.t.
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xAwalPage.Enabled=.t.
ENDIF
IF nMaxPage<=1
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xmajuPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xAkhirPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xmundurPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xAwalPage.Enabled=.f.
ENDIF 
xlimit="LIMIT "+ALLTRIM(STR(nFirstRow))+","+ALLTRIM(STR(nRowCount))
ENDPROC
PROCEDURE cari_jum_rec
PUBLIC nFirstRow,nRowCount,xlimit,nMaxPage,nTotRec,nMax_Row,xCurrentPage
*
XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,XJ1+XJ2,"TMP")
IF xh<>1 
   MESSAGEBOX("Database gagal diakses# !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   RETURN
ENDI 
IF USED("tmp")
  nTotRec = VAL(tmp.nTotRec)
  USE IN tmp
ELSE
  nTotRec = 0
ENDIF
thisform.pageframe1.page1.xrec.Value=nTotRec
thisform.pageframe1.page1.xcurrentPage.Value=1
thisform.pageframe1.page1.xPerPage.Value=200
ENDPROC
PROCEDURE buat_tmp_order
XFL="TMP_ORDBELI_T_"+ALLTRIM(LEFT(ZID,5))
XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT KODE_BRG FROM "+XFL+" LIMIT 1,1","CC")
IF XH=1
 
*FILE SUDAH ADA
ELSE
  Xt1="CREATE TABLE "+XFL+" (`F_ORDER` VARCHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`TGL_order` DATE NOT NULL,`CODESUP` VARCHAR(5) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`NAMA_SUP` VARCHAR(50) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',"
  XT2="`ALAMAT_SUP` VARCHAR(75) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`ACC` VARCHAR(3) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`NAMA_ACC` VARCHAR(30) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`TERSEDIA` DOUBLE(15,3) NOT NULL,"
  XT3="`HUTANG` CHAR(3) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`GRUP` CHAR(4) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`ISI` DOUBLE(10,3) NOT NULL,`JFPPN` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`QBELI` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`S_AKHIR` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,"
  XT4="`KODE_BRG` VARCHAR(10) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`NAMA_BRG` VARCHAR(50) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`SATUAN` CHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`DISC1` DOUBLE(6,2) NOT NULL, `DISC2` DOUBLE(6,2) NOT NULL,"
  XT5="`DISC3` DOUBLE(6,2) NOT NULL,`DISC_RP` DOUBLE(8,2) NOT NULL,`DISC_REG` DOUBLE(6,2) NOT NULL,`HRG_BELI` DOUBLE(15,2) NOT NULL,`JUMLAH` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`TUNAI` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`PPN` INTEGER(2) NOT NULL, `LAMA` DOUBLE(4,0) NOT NULL,"
  XT6="`OPR` VARCHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`DATEOPR` VARCHAR(16) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`BARCODE` VARCHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`URUTAN` INTEGER(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,"
  XT7="`NO_FAKTUR` VARCHAR(20) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`JML_TERIMA` DOUBLE(15,3) NOT NULL,`TGL_TERIMA` DATE NOT NULL,`OPR_TERIMA` VARCHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`QJUAL` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`JT_TEMPO` DATE NOT NULL,"
  XT8="`EST_ORDER` DOUBLE(15,3) NOT NULL,`BT1` DATE NOT NULL,`BQ1` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`BT2` DATE NOT NULL,`BQ2` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`BT3` DATE NOT NULL,`BQ3` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`F_BELI` VARCHAR(22) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',"
  xT9="`KET` VARCHAR(35) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`BONUS` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D1` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D2` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D3` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D4` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D_RET` DOUBLE(7,3) NOT NULL,"
  XT10="`DATEOPR_TERIMA` VARCHAR(20) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`TANDA` VARCHAR(1) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`CATATAN` VARCHAR(100) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`QRBELI` DOUBLE(15,3) NOT NULL,"
  XT11="PRIMARY KEY (`URUTAN`))ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=9820 CHARACTER SET 'utf8' COLLATE 'utf8_general_ci';"  
  XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,XT1+XT2+XT3+XT4+XT5+XT6+XT7+XT8+XT9+XT10+XT11)
  IF XH<>1
      MESSAGEBOX("CREATE FILE GAGAL !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
  ENDIF 
ENDIF   
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE cari_rec_artikel
PUBLIC nFirstRow,nRowCount,xlimit,nMaxPage,nTotRec,nMax_Row,xCurrentPage
STORE 0 TO nFirstRow,nRowCount,xlimit,nMaxPage,nTotRec,nMax_Row,xCurrentPage
*
XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,XJ1+XJ2,"TMP")
IF xh<>1 
   MESSAGEBOX("Database gagal diakses !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   RETURN
ENDI 
IF USED("tmp")
  COUNT TO NTOTREC 
  *nTotRec = VAL(tmp.nTotRec)
   USE IN tmp 
ELSE
  nTotRec = 0
ENDIF
thisform.pageframe1.page7.xrec.Value=nTotRec
thisform.pageframe1.page7.xcurrentPage.Value=1
thisform.pageframe1.page7.xPerPage.Value=200
ENDPROC
PROCEDURE cek_limit_artikel
nMax_Row=thisform.pageframe1.page7.xPerPage.Value
nMaxPage = INT((nTotRec + nMAX_ROW - 1) / nMAX_ROW)
thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xmaxPage.Value=nMaxPage
xCurrentPage=thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xCurrentPage.Value
nCurrentPage = MIN(MAX(xCurrentPage, 1), nMaxPage + 1)
thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xCurrentPage.Value=nCurrentPage
nFirstRow = (nCurrentPage - 1) * nMAX_ROW
IF (nFirstRow + nMAX_ROW) < nTotRec
   nRowCount = nMAX_ROW
ELSE
   nRowCount = MAX(nTotRec - nFirstRow, 0)
ENDIF
IF thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xcurrentPage.Value=thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xmaxPage.Value
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xmajuPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xAkhirPage.Enabled=.f.
else   
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xmajuPage.Enabled=.t.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xAkhirPage.Enabled=.t.
endi   
IF thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xcurrentPage.Value=1
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xmundurPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xAwalPage.Enabled=.f.
ELSE
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xmundurPage.Enabled=.t.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xAwalPage.Enabled=.t.
ENDIF
IF nMaxPage<=1
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xmajuPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xAkhirPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xmundurPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE7.xAwalPage.Enabled=.f.
ENDIF 
xlimit="LIMIT "+ALLTRIM(STR(nFirstRow))+","+ALLTRIM(STR(nRowCount))
ENDPROC

   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE9.xAwalPage.Enabled=.f.
ELSE
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE9.xmundurPage.Enabled=.t.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE9.xAwalPage.Enabled=.t.
ENDIF

   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE9.xmajuPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE9.xAkhirPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE9.xmundurPage.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.pageframe1.PAGE9.xAwalPage.Enabled=.f.
ENDIF

ENDPROC

PROCEDURE htg_order
SET DECIMALS TO 0
XA1=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XACUAN1.Value
XA2=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XACUAN2.Value
*MESSAGEBOX(ZOT)
XKODE=KODE_BRG
XHLD=HOLDING
XKETB=HB1
xrek=RECNO()
XST=.F.
STORE " " TO XBLN1,XBLN2,XBLN3,XBLN4,XBLN5,XBLN6,XBLN7,XBLN8,XBLN9,XBLN10,XBLN11,XBLN12
*
thisform.pageframe1.page1.container1.xPROMO.Value=" "
IF .not. EMPTY(no_promo)
   IF DATE()>=PR_TGL1 .and. DATE()<=PR_TGL2
    STORE " " TO xd1,xd2,xd3,xd4
    IF PR_disc1>0
       xd1="-"+ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(PR_disc1,"@Z99.99"))+"%"  
    endi   
    IF PR_disc2>0
       xd2="-"+ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(PR_disc2,"@Z99.99"))+"%"  
    endi   
    IF PR_disc3>0
       xd3="-"+ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(PR_disc3,"@Z99.99%"))+"%"  
    endi  
    IF PR_disc_rp>0
       xd4="-Rp."+ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(PR_disc_rp,"999,999"))  
    endi  
    thisform.pageframe1.page1.container1.xPROMO.Value=ALLTRIM(NO_PROMO)+"# "+DTOC(PR_TGL1)+"/"+DTOC(PR_TGL2)+"# Rp."+ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(PR_HARGA1,"99,999,999"))+ALLTRIM(xd1+Xd2+xd3+xd4) 
   ENDIF 
ENDI
*
STORE " " TO XKETJ,XKET,XBUL,XJUAL
*
xtglakhir=thisform.pageframe1.page1.container1.xaCUAN1.value
xawal    =thisform.pageframe1.page1.container1.xaCUAN2.Value
xHARI=XAWAL-XTGLAKHIR
YI=1
XKETJ=' '
XSALDO=0
XTJUAL=0
XTBL=0
XTRT=0
*
IF ZOT=0
    STORE " " TO xd1,xd2,xd3,xd4,xd5
    XSALDO=S_AKHIR
ELSE
   xrek=RECNO()
   SUM S_AKHIR TO XSALDO FOR kode_brg=xkode AND HOLDING=XHLD 
   IF XREK>0
      GO XREK
   ENDIF        
ENDIF 
IF !EMPTY(HB1)    
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XBELI_TGL.Value=HB1+CHR(13)+HB2+CHR(13)+HB3
ELSE
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XBELI_TGL.Value=" "
ENDIF 
IF !EMPTY(HJ1)    
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XJUAL_TGL.Value=HJ1
ELSE
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XJUAL_TGL.Value=" "
ENDIF 
IF !EMPTY(HO1)    
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XORDER_AKHIR.Value=HO1
ELSE
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XORDER_AKHIR.Value=" "
ENDIF 
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XSALDO.Value=XSALDO
IF !EMPTY(satuan2)
   XISI2=ISI2
   IF XSALDO>XISI2 
      IF ISI2>ISI1
         XKV=TRANSFORM(INT(XSALDO/XISI2),"9,999,999")+"-"+ALLTRIM(SATUAN2)
         thisform.pageframe1.page1.container1.xsA.Value=XKV
      ENDIF    
   ELSE
      THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XSA.Value=SATUAN1
   ENDI   
ELSE
    thisform.pageframe1.page1.container1.xsA.Value=SATUAN1
ENDIF 
*
*MESSAGEBOX(xawal)
*MESSAGEBOX(xtglakhir)
*retu
STORE 0 TO XTJUAL,XTMT
DO WHILE XAWAL>=XTGLAKHIR
  
       XJUAL=0
       XBL=0
       XRT=0
       XMT=0
   XB=DTOC(xAWAL)
   XN=SUBSTR(XB,4,2)
   XT=RIGHT(XB,4)
   XY=ALLTRIM(STR(YI))   
   XBLNTH=XN+XT
   
   IF XN='01'
      XBUL="JAN "+XT
      
      IF ZOT=0
         XJUAL=J_01
         xBL  =B_01
         XRT  =R_01
         XMT  =M_01
      ELSE
         xrek=RECNO()
         *XMT  =M_01
         SUM J_01 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XJUAL
         SUM B_01 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XBL
         SUM R_01 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XRT
    
         SUM M_01 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XMT
           
         IF XREK>0
   
GO XREK
 ENDIF 
      ENDIF 
   ENDIF    
   IF XN='02'
      XBUL ="FEB "+XT
      IF ZOT=0
         XJUAL=J_02
         xBL  =B_02
         XRT  =R_02
         XMT  =M_02
      ELSE
         xrek=RECNO()
         *XMT  =M_02
         SUM J_02 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XJUAL
         SUM B_02 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XBL
         SUM R_02 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XRT
         SUM M_02 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XMT
         
         IF XREK>0
   
GO XREK
 ENDIF 
      ENDIF 
   ENDIF    
   IF XN='03'
      XBUL ="MAR "+XT
     IF ZOT=0
         XJUAL=J_03
         xBL  =B_03
         XRT  =R_03
         XMT  =M_03
      ELSE
         xrek=RECNO()
         *XMT  =M_03
         SUM J_03 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XJUAL
         SUM B_03 FOR kode_brg=xkode .AND. HOLDING=XHLD TO XBL

   IF XN='04'

        XMT   =M_04
      ELSE

XORDER=XX
XPERHARI=(XTJUAL/XLAMA)  
xMG=XPERHARI*7
XSALDO=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XSaldo.Value
IF XSALDO>0 .AND. XPERHARI>0
   XTERSEDIA=INT(XSALDO/XPERHARI)
ELSE
   XTERSEDIA=0
ENDIF 
    *
   XD=VAL(LEFT(DTOC(DATE()),2))
   IF ZF_ORDER=2
   XY=0
   IF XD>=4 .AND. XD<=14
   XY=XORDER
   ENDIF    
   IF XD>=15 .AND. XD<=23
   XZO=INT(XORDER*(25/100))
   XY =XORDER-XZO
   ENDIF 
   IF XD>=24 .AND. XD<=31
   XZO=INT(XORDER*(25/100))
   XY =XORDER+XZO
   ENDIF 
   IF XD>=1 .AND. XD<=3
   XZO=INT(XORDER*(25/100))
   XY =XORDER+XZO
   ENDI
   XORDER=XY
   ENDI
   
*
   *THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XBULAN.VALUE='TOTAL'
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XHARI.Value=XLAMA
   *thisform.pageframe1.page1.CONtainer1.Xjual.Value=TRANSFORM(XTJUAL,"@Z999,999")   
*
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XRTJUALHR.Value=XPERHARI
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XTERSEDIA.Value=XTERSEDIA
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XBMG.Value=XORDER
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XMG.Value=XMG
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.grid1.SetFocus
SET DECIMALS TO 2
   
RETURN

thisform.pageframe1.ijin.xno_irt.Enabled=.t.
thisform.pageframe1.ijin.xno_halal.Enabled=.t.
thisform.pageframe1.ijin.xno_prd.Enabled=.t.

thisform.pageframe1.ijin.xno_irt.Enabled=.f.
thisform.pageframe1.ijin.xno_halal.Enabled=.f.

ENDPROC
PROCEDURE Destroy
USE IN BRG
USE IN ACC
USE IN DEPT
USE IN SUP
USE IN GRUP
ENDPROC
PROCEDURE Init
PUBLIC xds,xUBAH,XTAMBAH,XTAWAL,XFACC,XFBRG,zman,XCOPY,xst,ZHS,ZADD,ZEDIT,ZDEL,ZS_DATA,ZAKUN_HUTANG,ZPJ_KODE,ZF_ORDER,ZLONG_CODE,zART_KONTER,ZOT,XURUT,ZF_URUT
STORE 0 TO ZADD,ZEDIT,ZDEL,ZPJ_KODE,ZLONG_CODE,ZART_KONTER,ZOT,XURUT,XKD,ZF_URUT
XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT KODE,TAMBAH,UBAH,HAPUS FROM OTORITAS WHERE KODE='0109' AND USER_ID=?ZID AND XMODUL=1","AKSES")
IF XH<>1
   MESSAGEBOX("File Otoritas gagal dibuka !!")
   retu
endi   
SELECT AKSES
GO TOP
ZADD=TAMBAH
ZEDIT=UBAH
ZDEL=HAPUS
IF ZADD=1
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.TAMBAH.VISIBLE=.T.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.COMmand3.VISIBLE=.T.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.TAMBAH.VISIBLE=.T.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.SIMPAN.VISIBLE=.T.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page9.SIMPAN.VISIBLE=.T.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page8.SIMPAN.VISIBLE=.T.
ELSE     
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.TAMBAH.VISIBLE=.F.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.COMmand3.VISIBLE=.F.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.TAMBAH.VISIBLE=.F.    
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.SIMPAN.VISIBLE=.F. 
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page9.SIMPAN.VISIBLE=.F.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page8.SIMPAN.VISIBLE=.F.
ENDIF 
IF ZEDIT=1
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.Ubah.VISIBLE=.T.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.Ubah.VISIBLE=.T.     
   ELSE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.UBAH.VISIBLE=.F.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.UBAH.VISIBLE=.F.    
ENDIF 
IF ZDEL=1
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.Hapus.VISIBLE=.T.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.Hapus.VISIBLE=.T.
   ELSE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.HAPUS.VISIBLE=.F.
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.HAPUS.VISIBLE=.F.
ENDIF 
USE
xst=.t.
ZHS=.F.
SET DATE ITALIAN
SET CENTURY ON
SET score off
SET TALK OFF
SET EXACT ON
SET SAFETY ofF
*THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XMaxbln.Value=3
xMAXBLN=(THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XMaxbln.Value-1)
XMAX=DATE()-(xMaxBln*30)
xtglAWL=(xMAX-DAY(xMAX)+1)
*MESSAGEBOX(xTGLAWL)
XHARI=DATE()-XTGLAWL
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XACUAN1.Value=XTGLAWL
XACU=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XACUAN1.Value
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XHARI.Value=XHARI
XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,"SELECT ACC,NAMA_ACC FROM CBG_ACC ORDER BY ACC","HTGX")
IF xh<>1 
   MESSAGEBOX("Database CBG_ACC gagal diakses !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   RETURN

s-PROCEDURE Page1.Click
   
thisform.pageframe1.page1.SetFocus
    thisform.pageframe1.page1.grid1.SetFocus
ENDPROC
PROCEDURE Page2.Activate
IF ZADD=1
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page2.TAMBAH.Visible=.T.     
   ELSE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page2.TAMBAH.Visible=.F.     
ENDIF 
IF ZDEL=1
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page2.Hapus.Visible=.T.
   ELSE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page2.HAPUS.Visible=.F.
ENDIF 
*
XFS="TMP_SAT_"+ALLTRIM(LEFT(ZID,5))
XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT FSAT FROM "+XFS+" LIMIT 1,1","CC")
IF XH<>1
x1="CREATE TABLE "+xFS+" (`FSAT` CHAR(1) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`SATUAN` VARCHAR(10) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',"
    x2="`ISI` DOUBLE(7,2) NOT NULL,"
    x3=" FULLTEXT KEY `FSAT` (`FSAT`)) ENGINE=MyISAM CHARACTER SET 'utf8' COLLATE 'utf8_general_ci'; "
    XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+X2+X3)  
   IF XH<>1
  MESSAGEBOX("Create file SATUAN Gagal !!",0,"Perhatian !!")
  retu
   ENDIF   
ELSE 
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"DELETE FROM "+XFS) 
ENDIF
SELECT BRG
IF !EMPTY(SATUAN1)
   XFSAT="1"
   XSATUAN=ALLTRIM(SATUAN1)
   XISI=ISI1
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"INSERT INTO "+XFS+" (FSAT,SATUAN,ISI) VALUE (?XFSAT,?XSATUAN,?XISI)")
ENDIF
IF !EMPTY(SATUAN2)
   XFSAT="2"
   XSATUAN=ALLTRIM(SATUAN2)
   XISI=ISI2
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"INSERT INTO "+XFS+" (FSAT,SATUAN,ISI) VALUE (?XFSAT,?XSATUAN,?XISI)")
ENDIF
IF !EMPTY(SATUAN3)
   XFSAT="3"
   XSATUAN=ALLTRIM(SATUAN3)
   XISI=ISI3
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"INSERT INTO "+XFS+" (FSAT,SATUAN,ISI) VALUE (?XFSAT,?XSATUAN,?XISI)")
ENDIF
IF !EMPTY(SATUAN4)
   XFSAT="4"
   XSATUAN=ALLTRIM(SATUAN4)
   XISI=ISI4
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"INSERT INTO "+XFS+" (FSAT,SATUAN,ISI) VALUE (?XFSAT,?XSATUAN,?XISI)")
ENDIF
s1="SelecT * FROM "+XFS+" ORDER BY FSAT"
XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,S1,"SATX")
IF xh<>1 
   MESSAGEBOX("File temporer gagal dibuka!!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   RETURN
ENDI 
ENDPROC
PROCEDURE Page2.Click
XKD=BRG.KODE_bRG
xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT KODE_BRG,NAMA_BRG,SATUAN,BARCODE,UTGL,USER,ISI,FSAT,SP,URUTAN FROM FBARANG WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKD ORDER BY FSAT,URUTAN","FBARANG")
IF xh<>1 
   MESSAGEBOX("Database FBARANG gagal diakses !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
  RETURN
ENDI 
SELECT FBARANG
*BROWSE
GO TOP
thisform.browse_barcode
thisform.pageframe1.page2.GRid1.SetFocus
THISFORM.ISI_barcode
thisform.pageframe1.page2.tambah.Enabled=.t.
thisform.pageframe1.page2.simpan.Enabled=.f.
ENDPROC
PROCEDURE Page3.Deactivate
IF THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.xhRG_paket.Value<>THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.ZTJUAL.Value
   MESSAGEBOX("Total harga komposisi paket tidak sama dengan harga paket !!",0,"Perhatian !!")     
ENDIF    
ENDPROC
PROCEDURE Page3.Activate
IF ZADD=1
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.TAMBAH.Visible=.T.     
   ELSE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.TAMBAH.Visible=.F.     
ENDIF 
IF ZEDIT=1
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.Ubah.Visible=.T.
   ELSE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.UBAH.Visible=.F.
ENDIF 
IF ZDEL=1
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.Hapus.Visible=.T.
   ELSE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.HAPUS.Visible=.F.
ENDIF 
XACC=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XACC.Value
XNAMA_ACC=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XNAMA_ACC.VALUE
XKD=LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page1.xDEP.Value,2)+LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page1.xkoDE.Value,8)
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.xkode_paket.Value=xkd
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XNAMA_PAKET.Value=thisform.pageframe1.page1.xNAMA_BRG.Value
thisform.pageframe1.page3.xACC.Value=xacc
thisform.pageframe1.page3.xnAMA_ACC.Value=xnama_acc
xkode=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.xkode_paket.Value
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.xhRG_paket.Value=thisform.pageframe1.page1.xHRG_JUAL.Value
x1="SELECT DISTINCT paket.KODE_BRG,BARANG.NAMA_BRG,paket.HRG_BELI,paket.HRG_JUAL,paket.SATUAN,paket.JUMLAH,paket.ISI,paket.OPR,paket.DATEOPR,paket.FSAT,PAKET.URUTAN "
x2="FROM paket LEFT JOIN barang ON paket.KODE_BRG = BARANG.KODE_BRG AND PAKET.ACC=BARANG.ACC WHERE PAKET.KODE_PAKET=?XKD AND PAKET.ACC=?XACC "
x3="ORDER BY PAKET.KODE_PAKET"
xH=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+x2+x3,"PAKET")
IF xh<>1 
   MESSAGEBOX("Database KOMPOSISI gagal diakses !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   RETURN
ENDI 
SELECT PAKET
SUM HRG_JUAL*JUMLAH TO XJUAL
GO TOP
SUM HRG_BELI*JUMLAH TO XBELI
GO TOP
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.ZTBELI.Value=XBELI
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.ZTJUAL.VALUE=XJUAL
GO TOP
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XKODE_PAKET.Enabled=.F.
THISFORM.ISI_KOMPOSISI
thisform.browse_KOMPOSISI
thisform.pageframe1.page3.Grid1.SetFOCUS
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE Page4.Activate
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page4.XNAMA_BRG.Value=BRG.NAMA_BRG
thisform.pageframe1.page4.xkode_Brg.Value=brg.kode_Brg
XK=BRG.KODE_BRG
XA=BRG.ACC
XS="SELECT FGAMBAR FROM BARANG WHERE KODE_BRG=?XK AND ACC=?XA"
XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,XS,"GBR")
lfile =ZL_FOTO+ALLTRIM(GBR.FGAMBAR)
IF !EMPTY(LFILE)
IF FILE(LFILE)
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page4.Image1.Picture=LFILE
   
   thisform.pageframe1.page4.xnama_file.Caption=lfile
ELSE   
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page4.Image1.Picture=" "
ENDIF 
ENDI
thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE4.IMAGE1.Stretch= 2
USE IN GBR
ENDPROC

SELECT BRG
yACC=BRG.ACC

ys1="SELECT SATUAN1,isi1,qty11,harga11,qty12,harga12,qty13,harga13,harga1A,harga1B," 
ys2="SATUAN2,isi2,qty21,harga21,qty22,harga22,qty23,harga23,harga2A,harga2B," 
ys3="SATUAN3,isi3,qty31,harga31,qty32,harga32,qty33,harga33,harga3A,harga3B," 
ys4="SATUAN4,isi4,qty41,harga41,qty42,harga42,qty43,harga43,harga4A,harga4B,disc,URUTAN," 
yS5="HARGA1C,HARGA2C,HARGA3C,HARGA4C,profit,PROFIT_1A FROM barang WHERE ACC=?yACC AND KODE_BRG=?yKODE_BRG"
xH=SQLEXEC(XDS,yS1+yS2+yS3+yS4+yS5,"GR")

   MESSAGEBOX("Database BARANG gagal diakses !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   RETURN
ENDI

   IF XHARGA11>0
  xreal=((Xharga11/XHPP)*100)-100
   ELSE
  XREAL=0
   ENDIF    
ELSE   
   XREAL=0
ENDI     
thisform.pageframe1.page5.xPH11.Value=XREAL

   IF XHARGA12>0
  xreal=((Xharga12/XHPP)*100)-100
   ELSE
  XREAL=0
   ENDIF    
ELSE   
   XREAL=0
ENDI     
thisform.pageframe1.page5.xPH12.Value=XREAL

   IF XHARGA13>0

   ELSE
  XREAL=0
   ENDIF    
ELSE

PROCEDURE Page10.Activate
PUBLIC XMREK
SELECT BRG
XMREK=0
IF RECNO()>0
  XMREK=RECNO()
ENDIF 
XFL="TMP_ORDBELI_T_"+ALLTRIM(LEFT(ZID,5))
*
XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT KODE_BRG FROM "+XFL+" LIMIT 1,1","CC")
IF XH=1
 
*FILE SUDAH ADA
 
SELECT cc
 
USE IN cc
ELSE
  Xt1="CREATE TABLE "+XFL+" (`F_ORDER` VARCHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`TGL_order` DATE NOT NULL,`CODESUP` VARCHAR(5) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`NAMA_SUP` VARCHAR(50) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',"
  XT2="`ALAMAT_SUP` VARCHAR(75) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`ACC` VARCHAR(3) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`NAMA_ACC` VARCHAR(30) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`TERSEDIA` DOUBLE(15,3) NOT NULL,"
  XT3="`HUTANG` CHAR(3) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`GRUP` CHAR(4) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`ISI` DOUBLE(10,3) NOT NULL,`JFPPN` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`QBELI` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`S_AKHIR` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,"
  XT4="`KODE_BRG` VARCHAR(10) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`NAMA_BRG` VARCHAR(50) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`SATUAN` CHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`DISC1` DOUBLE(6,2) NOT NULL, `DISC2` DOUBLE(6,2) NOT NULL,"
  XT5="`DISC3` DOUBLE(6,2) NOT NULL,`DISC_RP` DOUBLE(8,2) NOT NULL,`DISC_REG` DOUBLE(6,2) NOT NULL,`HRG_BELI` DOUBLE(15,2) NOT NULL,`JUMLAH` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`TUNAI` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`PPN` INTEGER(2) NOT NULL, `LAMA` DOUBLE(4,0) NOT NULL,"
  XT6="`OPR` VARCHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`DATEOPR` VARCHAR(16) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`BARCODE` VARCHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`URUTAN` INTEGER(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,"
  XT7="`NO_FAKTUR` VARCHAR(20) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`JML_TERIMA` DOUBLE(15,3) NOT NULL,`TGL_TERIMA` DATE NOT NULL,`OPR_TERIMA` VARCHAR(15) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`QJUAL` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`JT_TEMPO` DATE NOT NULL,"
  XT8="`EST_ORDER` DOUBLE(15,3) NOT NULL,`BT1` DATE NOT NULL,`BQ1` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`BT2` DATE NOT NULL,`BQ2` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`BT3` DATE NOT NULL,`BQ3` DOUBLE(15,0) NOT NULL,`F_BELI` VARCHAR(22) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',"
  xT9="`KET` VARCHAR(35) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`BONUS` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D1` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D2` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D3` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D4` INTEGER(1) NOT NULL,`D_RET` DOUBLE(7,3) NOT NULL,"
  XT10="`DATEOPR_TERIMA` VARCHAR(20) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`TANDA` VARCHAR(1) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`CATATAN` VARCHAR(100) COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',`QRBELI` DOUBLE(15,3) NOT NULL,"
  XT11="PRIMARY KEY (`URUTAN`))ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=9820 CHARACTER SET 'utf8' COLLATE 'utf8_general_ci';"  
  XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,XT1+XT2+XT3+XT4+XT5+XT6+XT7+XT8+XT9+XT10+XT11)
  IF XH<>1
      MESSAGEBOX("CREATE FILE GAGAL !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
  ENDIF
ENDIF   
*
X1="SELECT KODE_BRG,NAMA_BRG,SATUAN,"
X2="JUMLAH,HRG_BELI,DISC1,DISC2,DISC3,DISC_RP,BONUS,KET,D1,D2,D3,D4,PPN "
X3="FROM "+XFL+" order by URUTAN"
XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,X1+X2+X3,"ORDX")
IF xh<>1 
   MESSAGEBOX("Database DORX gagal diakses !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   RETUR
ENDI   
SELECT ORDX
GO TOP
STORE 0 TO XTFAK,XFAK,XJPPN,XTNFAK
DO WHILE .NOT. EOF()
      xDISC1=DISC1
      XDISC2=DISC2
      XDISC3=DISC3
      XDISC_RP=DISC_RP
      XJUMLAH=JUMLAH
      XHRG_BELI=HRG_BELI
      XPPN=PPN
      STORE 0 TO XN1,XN2,XN3,XN4,XD_FAK,XD_NFAK
      IF D1=1         
         XDISC1=0   
         XN1=DISC1     
      ENDIF 
      IF D2=1
         XDISC2=0
         XN2=DISC2     
      ENDIF 
      IF D3=1
         XDISC3=0
         XN3=DISC3     
      ENDIF 
      IF D4=1
         XDISC_RP=0
         XN4=DISC_RP    
      ENDIF 
      XPOKOK =(XJUMLAH*XHRG_BELI)
      XFAK=(XJUMLAH*XHRG_BELI*((100-XDISC1)/100)*((100-XDISC2)/100)*((100-XDISC3)/100))-(XDISC_RP*XJUMLAH)
      XD_FAK= XPOKOK - XFAK
      *
      XNFAK  =(XFAK*((100-XN1)/100)*((100-XN2)/100)*((100-XN3)/100))-(XN4*XJUMLAH)
      XD_NFAK=XFAK-XNFAK
      XTNFAK = XTNFAK + XD_NFAK
      XTFAK  =  XTFAK + XFAK
      XJPPN =  XJPPN + (XFAK*(XPPN/100))                
    SKIP 
ENDD 
THISFORM.Pageframe1.PAGE10.Xtotal.value=xTFAK
GO top
*BROWSE
thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE10.grid1.RecordSource="ORDX"
thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE10.grid1.RecordSourceType=1
thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE10.grid1.FontSize=10

   MESSAGEBOX("Kode tidak boleh kosong !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xdep.SetFocus
   RETURN
endi   
IF Xnama_brg=" " 
   MESSAGEBOX("Nama barang tidak boleh kosong !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xnama_brg.SetFocus
   RETURN
endi   
IF XSATUAN=" " 
   MESSAGEBOX("Satuan barang tidak boleh kosong !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xsatuan.SetFocus
   RETURN
endi   
IF XISI1=0 .OR. EMPTY(XSATUAN1)
   MESSAGEBOX("SATUAN1/ISI1 harus diisi !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xisi1.SetFocus
   RETURN
endi   
IF !EMPTY(XSATUAN2)
   IF XISI2=0
      MESSAGEBOX("Isi SATUAN2 barang tidak boleh 0 (nol) !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
      thisform.pageframe1.page1.xisi2.SetFocus
      RETURN
   ENDIF    
endi   
IF !EMPTY(XSATUAN3)
   IF XISI3=0
      MESSAGEBOX("Isi SATUAN3 barang tidak boleh 0 (nol) !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
      thisform.pageframe1.page1.xisi3.SetFocus
      RETURN
   ENDIF    
endi   
IF !EMPTY(XSATUAN4)
   IF XISI4=0
      MESSAGEBOX("Isi SATUAN4 barang tidak boleh 0 (nol) !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
      thisform.pageframe1.page1.xisi4.SetFocus
      RETURN
   ENDIF    
endi   
    IF XCOPY .OR. XTAMBAH
       XAC=LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page1.xACC.Value,3)
       XKD=ALLTRIM(thisform.pageframe1.page1.xdep.Value)+LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page1.xkoDE.Value,7)
       sqlexec(xds,"select * from BARANG where ACC=?XAC AND KODE_BRG=?xKD order by KODE_BRG","CC")
   SELECT CC
   IF !EMPTY(CC.KODE_BRG)
      use
      MESSAGEBOX("Kode Barang tersebut sudah terdaftar/double !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
      thisform.pageframe1.page1.xACC.SetFocus
      RETURN
   ENDI   
   USE
 ENDIF  
IF XCOPY  
       
       XACC=LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page1.xACC.Value,3)
       XNAMA_ACC=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XNAMA_ACC.Value
       xuser=DTOC(DATE())+TIME()       
       SELECT BRG
       XAC=ACC
       xkb=kode_Brg
       XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT * FROM BARANG WHERE ACC=?XAC AND KODE_BRG=?XKB","CR")
       SELECT CR
       IF !EMPTY(CR.KODE_BRG)
           XSYN=1           
       x1="insert into BARANG (acc,NAMA_ACC,kode_brg,nama_brg,codesup,satuan,HET,s_awal,s_akhir,stock,paket,grup,HRG_BELI,PAJAK,FGAMBAR,HPP_AKHIR,USER,UTGL,"
       X2="DISAMAKAN,NAMA_GRUP,NAMA_DEP,SUB_MERK,NAMA_MERK,NAMA_SUP,PROFIT,NON_AKTIF,NO_PROMO,MIX_GROSIR,P_MEMBER,LOKASI,HOLDING,TGL_BUAT,KONSI,HUTANG,BI_LISTING,"
       X3="SATUAN1,ISI1,QTY11,HARGA11,QTY12,HARGA12,QTY13,HARGA13,HARGA1A,HARGA1B,SATUAN2,ISI2,QTY21,HARGA21,QTY22,HARGA22,QTY23,HARGA23,HARGA2A,HARGA2B,"
       X4="SATUAN3,ISI3,QTY31,HARGA31,QTY32,HARGA32,QTY33,HARGA33,HARGA3A,HARGA3B,SATUAN4,ISI4,QTY41,HARGA41,QTY42,HARGA42,QTY43,HARGA43,HARGA4A,HARGA4B,SYN,N_EXP) "  
       x5="VALUES (?XACC,?XNAMA_ACC,?Xkode_brg,?CR.nama_brg,?CR.codesup,?CR.satuan,?CR.HET,0,0,?cr.stock,?cr.paket,?cr.grup,?cr.HRG_BELI,?cr.PAJAK,?cr.FGAMBAR,?cr.HPP_AKHIR,?xUSER,?xUTGL,"
       X6="?CR.DISAMAKAN,?CR.NAMA_GRUP,?CR.NAMA_DEP,?CR.SUB_MERK,?CR.NAMA_MERK,?CR.NAMA_SUP,?CR.PROFIT,?CR.NON_AKTIF,?CR.NO_PROMO,?CR.MIX_GROSIR,?CR.P_MEMBER,?CR.LOKASI,?XHLD,?XTGL_BUAT,?CR.KONSI,?CR.HUTANG,?XBI_LISTING,"
       X7="?CR.satuan1,?CR.ISI1,?CR.QTY11,?CR.HARGA11,?CR.QTY12,?CR.HARGA12,?CR.QTY13,?CR.HARGA13,?CR.HARGA1A,?CR.HARGA1B,?CR.SATUAN2,?CR.ISI2,?CR.QTY21,?CR.HARGA21,?CR.QTY22,?CR.HARGA22,?CR.QTY23,?CR.HARGA23,?CR.HARGA2A,?CR.HARGA2B,"
   X8="?CR.SATUAN3,?CR.ISI3,?CR.QTY31,?CR.HARGA31,?CR.QTY32,?CR.HARGA32,?CR.QTY33,?CR.HARGA33,?CR.HARGA3A,?CR.HARGA3B,?CR.SATUAN4,?CR.ISI4,?CR.QTY41,?CR.HARGA41,?CR.QTY42,?CR.HARGA42,?CR.QTY43,?CR.HARGA43,?CR.HARGA4A,?CR.HARGA4B,?XSYN,?XN_EXP)"
       Xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+X2+X3+X4+X5+X6+X7+X8)            
       IF xh<>1
      MESSAGEBOX("Record file BARANG gagal DICOPYKAN !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
       ENDIF  
   ENDI    
       SELECT BRG
    ENDIF    
    *
    IF XTAMBAH         
       IF !EMPTY(xkode_brg)
           XSYN=1
   x1="insert into BARANG (acc,kode_brg,nama_brg,codesup,satuan,HET,s_awal,s_akhir,stock,paket,grup,HRG_BELI,SATUAN1,HARGA11,PAJAK,HPP_AKHIR,USER,UTGL,SATUAN2,SATUAN3,SATUAN4,ISI1,ISI2,ISI3,ISI4,SUB_MERK,MAX_STOCK,MIN_STOCK,"
   x2="nama_sup,nama_acc,nama_grup,nama_merk,nama_dep,expired,profit,QTY11,DISAMAKAN,CATATAN,KONSI,NON_AKTIF,NO_PROMO,MIX_GROSIR,P_MEMBER,LOKASI,TGL_BUAT,HUTANG,HOLDING,SYN,N_EXP,BI_LISTING) "
   x3="VALUES (?Xacc,?Xkode_brg,?Xnama_brg,?Xcodesup,?Xsatuan,?XHET,?Xs_awal,?Xs_akhir,?Xstock,?xpaket,?xgrup,?XHRG_BELI,?XSATUAN1,?XHARGA11,?XPAJAK,?XHPP_AKHIR,?XUSER,?XUTGL,?XSATUAN2,?XSATUAN3,?XSATUAN4,?XISI1,?XISI2,?XISI3,?XISI4,"
   x4="?XSUB_MERK,?XMAX_STOCK,?XMIN_STOCK,?xnama_sup,?xnama_acc,?xnama_grup,?xnama_merk,?xnama_dep,?xEXPIRED,?xprofit,?XQTY11,?XDISAMAKAN,?XCATATAN,?xkonsi,?XAKTIF,?XNO_PROMO,?XMIX_GROSIR,?XP_MEMBER,?XLOKASI,?XTGL_BUAT,?XHUTANG,?XHLD,?XSYN,?XN_EXP,?XBI_LISTING)"
 
   xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+X2+x3+x4)
   IF xh<>1
   
 
   
  MESSAGEBOX("Data gagal disimpanxx !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
   endi   
ENDIF    
 ENDIF 
 IF XUBAH
   SELECT BRG
   XURUT=BRG.URUTAN
   xk=BRG.kode_brg
   XD=BRG.DISAMAKAN
   xa=brg.acc
   XSYN=1
   x1="UPDATE barang SET HET=?xHET,s_awal=?xs_awal,s_akhir=?xs_awal+q_beli-q_rbeli-q_jual+q_rjual-q_pakai-q_hapus+q_trf+q_opname+Q_PKODE,HPP_AKHIR=?xhpp_akhir,MAX_STOCK=?XMAX_STOCK,MIN_STOCK=?XMIN_STOCK,DISAMAKAN=?XDISAMAKAN,s_akhir=?xs_akhir,"
   x2="HARGA11=?xharga11,PROFIT=?XPROFIT,USER=?XUSER,UTGL=?XUTGL,LOKASI=?XLOKASI,TGL_BUAT=?XTGL_BUAT,NON_AKTIF=?XAKTIF,HOLDING=?XHLD,SYN=?XSYN WHERE KODE_BRG=?XK and ACC=?XA"
   xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+X2)
   
   IF xh<>1
      MESSAGEBOX("Data BARANG Gagal diubah !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
      THISFORM.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.SIMpan.SetFocus
      RETU
   ENDIF
   IF xdisamakan=1
      x1="UPDATE barang SET HARGA11=?xharga11,Profit=?xProfit,NON_AKTIF=?XAKTIF "
  x2="WHERE KODE_BRG=?XK and disamakan=1"
  xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+X2)
   
  IF xh<>1
     MESSAGEBOX("Data BARANG Gagal diubah !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
 THISFORM.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.SIMpan.SetFocus
 RETU
  ENDIF
   
   ENDIF 
   
   
   IF ZART_KONTER=0
   x1="UPDATE barang SET nama_brg=?xnama_brg,codesup=?xcodesup,satuan=?xsatuan,stock=?xstock,ISI1=?XISI1,ISI2=?XISI2,ISI3=?XISI3,ISI4=?XISI4,HRG_BELI=?xhrg_beli,CATATAN=?XCATATAN,USER=?XUSER,UTGL=?XUTGL,P_MEMBER=?XP_MEMBER,"
   x2="paket=?xpaket,grup=?xgrup,SATUAN1=?xsatuan1,PAJAK=?xpajak,SATUAN2=?XSATUAN2,SATUAN3=?XSATUAN3,SATUAN4=?XSATUAN4,SUB_MERK=?XSUB_MERK,HET=?xHET,HPP_AKHIR=?xhpp_akhir,NO_PENDING=?XNO_PENDING,MIX_GROSIR=?XMIX_GROSIR,"
   x3="nama_sup=?xnama_sup,nama_acc=?xnama_acc,nama_grup=?xnama_grup,nama_merk=?xnama_merk,nama_dep=?xnama_dep,ExPIRED=?XEXPIRED,KONSI=?xkonsi,HUTANG=?XHUTANG,N_EXP=?XN_EXP,BI_LISTING=?xBI_LISTING WHERE KODE_BRG=?XK "
   ELSE
       x1="UPDATE barang SET nama_brg=?xnama_brg,codesup=?xcodesup,satuan=?xsatuan,stock=?xstock,ISI1=?XISI1,ISI2=?XISI2,ISI3=?XISI3,ISI4=?XISI4,HRG_BELI=?xhrg_beli,CATATAN=?XCATATAN,USER=?XUSER,UTGL=?XUTGL,P_MEMBER=?XP_MEMBER,"
       x2="paket=?xpaket,grup=?xgrup,SATUAN1=?xsatuan1,PAJAK=?xpajak,SATUAN2=?XSATUAN2,SATUAN3=?XSATUAN3,SATUAN4=?XSATUAN4,SUB_MERK=?XSUB_MERK,HET=?xHET,HPP_AKHIR=?xhpp_akhir,NO_PENDING=?XNO_PENDING,MIX_GROSIR=?XMIX_GROSIR,"
       x3="nama_sup=?xnama_sup,nama_acc=?xnama_acc,nama_grup=?xnama_grup,nama_merk=?xnama_merk,nama_dep=?xnama_dep,ExPIRED=?XEXPIRED,KONSI=?xkonsi,HUTANG=?XHUTANG,N_EXP=?XN_EXP,BI_LISTING=?xBI_LISTING WHERE KODE_BRG=?XK AND ACC=?XA"
   ENDI
   xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+X2+x3)
   
   IF xh<>1
      MESSAGEBOX("Data Gagal diubah !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
      THISFORM.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.SIMpan.SetFocus
      RETU
   ENDIF
   IF xall_ppn=1
      x1= "update BARANG set PAJAK=?xpajak where codesup=?xcodesup"
      
      xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1)
      IF xh<>1
   
 
   
         MESSAGEBOX("Gagal update pajak persupplier !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
      endi  
   ENDIF 
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.Tambah.SetFocus
 ENDIF
 xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT KODE_BRG FROM FBARANG WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKODE_BRG ORDER BY KODE_BRG,FSAT","FBR")
 IF xh<>1
   
 
   
    MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode gagal dibuka !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
 endi  
 SELECT fbr 
 GO top
 IF EMPTY(fbr.kode_brg)
    USE
    * BARCODE DEFAULT
    XFSAT="1"
    XSYN=1
    x1= "insert into FBARANG (kode_brg,nama_brg,BARCODE,FSAT,SATUAN,USER,UTGL,ISI,SYN) VALUES "
    x2="(?Xkode_brg,?Xnama_brg,?XBARCODE,?XFSAT,?XSATUAN,?XUSER,?XUTGL,?XISI1,?XSYN)"
 
    xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+X2)
    IF xh<>1
   
 
   
       MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
    ENDIF
  
      
 else      
     use   
     IF !EMPTY(XSATUAN1) 
         XFSAT="1"
         x1= "update FBARANG set nama_brg=?xnama_brg,SATUAN=?XSATUAN1,USER=?XUSER,UTGL=?XUTGL,ISI=?XISI1 where kode_brg=?xkode_brg AND FSAT=?XFSAT"
      
         xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1)
         IF xh<>1
   
 
   
            MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
         endi  
     ENDI    
     IF !EMPTY(XSATUAN2) 
         XFSAT="2"
         x1= "update FBARANG set nama_brg=?xnama_brg,SATUAN=?XSATUAN2,USER=?XUSER,UTGL=?XUTGL,ISI=?XISI2 where kode_brg=?xkode_brg AND FSAT=?XFSAT"
      
         xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1)
         IF xh<>1
   
 
   
            MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
         endi  
     ENDI   
     IF !EMPTY(XSATUAN3) 
         XFSAT="3"
         x1= "update FBARANG set nama_brg=?xnama_brg,SATUAN=?XSATUAN3,USER=?XUSER,UTGL=?XUTGL,ISI=?XISI3 where kode_brg=?xkode_brg AND FSAT=?XFSAT"
      
         xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1)
         IF xh<>1
   
 
   
            MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
         endi  
     ENDI     
      IF !EMPTY(XSATUAN4) 
         XFSAT="4"
         x1= "update FBARANG set nama_brg=?xnama_brg,SATUAN=?XSATUAN4,USER=?XUSER,UTGL=?XUTGL,ISI=?XISI4 where kode_brg=?xkode_brg AND FSAT=?XFSAT"
      
         xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1)
         IF xh<>1
   
 
   
            MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
         endi  
     ENDI   
     
 ENDIF
*
IF XTAMBAH
xJ1="SELECT COUNT(*) AS nTotRec FROM barang"
    XJ2=" "
THISFORM.CARI_jum_rec
THISFORM.CEk_limit
xs1="SELECT ACC,KODE_BRG,NAMA_BRG,S_AKHIR,CODESUP,harga11,HARGA1A,(Q_JUAL-Q_RJUAL),Q_BELI,Q_RBELI,HOLDING,USER,UTGL,GRUP,HET,HPP_AKHIR,SATUAN,"
xs2="SUB_MERK,NAMA_MERK,PROFIT,HRG_BELI,DISC,STOCK,S_AWAL,PAKET,SATUAN1,ISI1,SATUAN2,ISI2,SATUAN3,MAX_STOCK,NON_AKTIF,tgl_buat,kode_lama,"
xs3="ISI3,SATUAN4,ISI4,KONSI,NON_AKTIF,pajak,LOKASI,URUTAN,NAMA_ACC,NAMA_SUP,MIN_STOCK,NAMA_DEP,DISAMAKAN,CATATAN,KONSI,P_MEMBER,"
xs4="NAMA_GRUP,expired,JUAL_TGL,BELI_TGL,BELI_SUP,BELI_HRG,BELI_D1,BELI_D2,BELI_D3,BELI_DRP,MIX_GROSIR,P_MEMBER,N_EXP,NO_IRT,NO_PRD,NO_HALAL,CAT_KOMPOSISI,"
xs5="J_01,J_02,J_03,J_04,J_05,J_06,J_07,J_08,J_09,J_10,J_11,J_12,JUAL_TGL,BELI_TGL,BELI_SAT,HRG_ORDER,HUTANG,HPP_NET,BI_LISTING,HO1,"
xs6="B_01,B_02,B_03,B_04,B_05,B_06,B_07,B_08,B_09,B_10,B_11,B_12,HB1,HB2,HB3,HJ1,qty11,qty21,harga21,qty31,harga31,qty41,harga41,"
xs7="R_01,R_02,R_03,R_04,R_05,R_06,R_07,R_08,R_09,R_10,R_11,R_12,qty12,harga12,qty13,harga13,qty22,harga22,qty23,harga23,qty32,harga32,qty33,harga33,qty42,harga42,qty43,harga43,disc,"
XS8="NO_PROMO,PR_TGL1,PR_TGL2,PR_HARGA1,PR_DISC1,PR_DISC2,PR_DISC3,PR_DISC_RP,M_01,M_02,M_03,M_04,M_05,M_06,M_07,M_08,M_09,M_10,M_11,M_12 "
XS9="FROM barang order by KODE_BRG,ACC "
ENDI
THISFORM.Pageframe1.page1.xALL_PPN.Visible=.T.
thisform.pageframe1.page1.xall_PPN.Value=0
IF !xubah
   
   XDEP=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XDEP.Value
   XKODE=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XKODE.Value
   XSM=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XSUB_MERK.Value
   
   XNMK=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XNAMA_MERK.Value
   XCODESUP=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XCODESUP.Value
   XNAMA_SUP=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XNAMASUP.Value
   XDISAMAKAN=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XDISAMAKAN.Value
   thisform.kosong
     
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.tambah.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.ubah.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.simpan.Enabled=.t.
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.hapus.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.batal.Enabled=.t.
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XHRG_JUAL.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XHPP.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XHET.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XPROFIT.Value=XPR
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XHRG_JUAL.Value=XHJ
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XHRG_BELI.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XS_AWAL.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XS_AKHIR.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XMIN_stock.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XMax_stock.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XDEP.Value=XDP
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XNAMA_DEP.Value=xND
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XKODE.Value=XKOD
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XNAMA_BRG.Value=XNB
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XDEP.Value=XDEP
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XKODE.Value=XKODE
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.XSUB_MERK.Value=XSM
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.XNAMA_MERK.Value=XNMK
   
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XNAMAGROUP.Value=XNG
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.XGROUP.Value=XGR
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XCODESUP.Value=XCODESUP
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XNAMASUP.Value=XNAMA_SUP
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XDISAMAKAN.Value=XDISAMAKAN
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.XACC.SetFocus
ELSE
  thisform.buka_barang
  SELECT BRG
  thisform.browse_data
 
  THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.Grid1.Refresh
  thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE1.grid1.FontBold= .T.
  LOCATE FOR URUTAN=XURUT
  THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.Grid1.SetFocus
 
  THISFORM.Pageframe1.PAge1.Ubah.Enabled=.T. 
ENDIF
xubah=.f.
XCOPY=.F.
ENDPROC

commandbutton
hapus
Form1.Pageframe1.Page1
Top = 584
Left = 275
Height = 53
Width = 88
FontBold = .T.
FontSize = 12
Picture = wzdelete.bmp
Caption = "\<Hapus"
TabIndex = 105
Name = "hapus"
PROCEDURE Click
thisform.pageframe1.page1.tambah.Enabled=.f.
thisform.pageframe1.page1.simpan.Enabled=.f.
thisform.pageframe1.page1.batal.Enabled=.t.
thisform.pageframe1.page1.hapus.Enabled=.T.
thisform.pageframe1.page1.ubah.Enabled=.f.
xacc=thisform.pageframe1.page1.XACC.Value
xdep=ALLTRIM(thisform.pageframe1.page1.XDEP.Value)
xkode=LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page1.XKODE.Value,7)
xkode_brg=xdep+xkode
IF RECCOUNT()=0
   MESSAGEBOX("Tidak ada data yang dihapus!!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.tambah.SetFocus
   RETURN 
ENDIF
SELECT BRG
XURUTAN=BRG.URUTAN
XKD=KODE_BRG
xrek=RECNO()
xC=ACC
if messagebox("Yakin ' "+Xkode_brg+"' akan dihapus..?",4+32+256,"Perhatian")=6
   XH=sqlexec(xds,"delete from BARANG where URUTAN=?XURUTAN")
   IF xh<>1 
      MESSAGEBOX("Data Gagal dihapus !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
      RETURN
   ELSE
      SQLEXEC(XDS,"ALTER TABLE BARANG AUTO_INCREMENT=0")  
      XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,"SELECT KODE_BRG FROM BARANG WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKD","XX")
      SELECT XX
      IF EMPTY(KODE_BRG)
     XH=sqlexec(xds,"Delete from FBARANG where kode_brg=?xKD")
 IF xh<>1 
     MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode Gagal dihapus !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
     RETURN
 ENDI    
 SQLEXEC(XDS,"ALTER TABLE FBARANG AUTO_INCREMENT=0")
  ENDIF 
  
  MESSAGEBOX("Kode barang : "+ALLTRIM(XKD)+" - "+ALLTRIM(xc)+" telah dihapus..Refresh untuk perubahan dilayar !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")              
   ENDI 
ENDI   
SELECT BRG
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.Grid1.SetFocus
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE GotFocus
IF !XUBAH
    XCARI=LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page1.xdep.Value,ZL_DEP)
    sqlexec(xds,"select * from DEPT where KODE_DEPT=?xcari order by KODE_DEPT","CARIZ")
SELECT CARIZ
IF KODE_DEPT=" "
   use
   MESSAGEBOX("Kode Departemen belum terdaftar !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xdep.SetFocus
   RETURN
ELSE
   IF F_LISTING=1
      MESSAGEBOX("Pendaftaran harus listing pusat !!",0,"Perhatian !!")
      thisform.pageframe1.page1.xdEP.Value=" "
      thisform.pageframe1.page1.xdep.SetFocus
      retu
    
   ELSE
  THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XNAMA_DEP.Value=CARIZ.NAMA_DEPT
  USE 
  thisform.pageframe1.page1.xKODE.SetFocus
   ENDIF 
ENDIF
ELSE
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.XKODE.SetFocus
ENDIF    
ENDPROC

   *MESSAGEBOX(XLONG)
   *MESSAGEBOX(XDATACARI)
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,XS1+XS2+XS3+XS4+XS5+XS6+XS7+XS8+XS9,"BRG")

XA2=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XACUAN2.Value
*XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SHOW DATABASES LIKE '"+XDB+"'","XX")
*XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"USE INV032018","XX")
*MESSAGEBOX(Xa1)
*MESSAGEBOX(Xa2)
SELECT BRG
XKODE=KODE_BRG
XST=.F.
xac=thisform.pageframe1.page1.container1.xACC.Value
IF EMPTY(ALLTRIM(xac))
  * MESSAGEBOX(XA1)
  * MESSAGEBOX(XA2)
  * MESSAGEBOX(XKODE)
  * MESSAGEBOX(XDS)
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT TGL_JUAL,JUMLAH,HRG_JUAL,DISC1,DISC2,DISC3,DISC_RP,ISI,KODE_SLS FROM DJUAL WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKODE AND TGL_JUAL>=?XA1 AND TGL_JUAL<=?XA2 ORDER BY TGL_JUAL DESC ","JUALX")
   SELECT JUALX
   *BROWSE
ELSE
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT TGL_JUAL,JUMLAH,HRG_JUAL,DISC1,DISC2,DISC3,DISC_RP,ISI,KODE_SLS FROM DJUAL WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKODE and ACC=?XAC AND TGL_JUAL>=?XA1 AND TGL_JUAL<=?XA2 ORDER BY TGL_JUAL DESC ","JUALX")
ENDIF    
IF XH<>1
   MESSAGEBOX("File DJual Gagal dibuka !!",0,"Perhatian !!")
   retu
ENDIF

   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI3.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI3,"@Z999,999")
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI4.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI4,"@Z999,999")
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI5.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI5,"@Z999,999")
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI6.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI6,"@Z999,999")
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI7.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI7,"@Z999,999")
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI8.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI8,"@Z999,999")
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI9.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI9,"@Z999,999")
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI10.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI10,"@Z999,999")
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI11.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI11,"@Z999,999")
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONTAINER1.XRBELI12.Value=TRANSFORM(XRBELI12,"@Z999,999")
   *
   XTJUAL =XJUAL0+XJUAL1+XJUAL2+XJUAL3+XJUAL4+XJUAL5+XJUAL6+XJUAL7+XJUAL8+XJUAL9+XJUAL10+XJUAL11+XJUAL12
   XTBELI =XBELI0+XBELI1+XBELI2+XBELI3+XBELI4+XBELI5+XBELI6+XBELI7+XBELI8+XBELI9+XBELI10+XBELI11+XBELI12
   XTRBELI=XRBELI0+XRBELI1+XRBELI2+XRBELI3+XRBELI4+XRBELI5+XRBELI6+XRBELI7+XRBELI8+XRBELI9+XRBELI10+XRBELI11+XRBELI12
   XTBELI =(XTBELI-XTRBELI)
   xlama=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XACUAN2.Value-THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XACUAN1.Value
   XX =INT((XTJUAL/XLAMA)*10)
   XORDER=XX
   XPERHARI=(XTJUAL/XLAMA)  
   xMG=XPERHARI*7
   XSALDO=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XSaldo.Value
   IF XSALDO>0 .AND. XPERHARI>0
      XTERSEDIA=INT(XSALDO/XPERHARI)
   ELSE
      XTERSEDIA=0
   ENDIF 
    *
   XD=VAL(LEFT(DTOC(DATE()),2))
   IF ZF_ORDER=2
   XY=0
   IF XD>=4 .AND. XD<=14
   XY=XORDER
   ENDIF    
   IF XD>=15 .AND. XD<=23
   XZO=INT(XORDER*(25/100))
   XY =XORDER-XZO
   ENDIF 
   IF XD>=24 .AND. XD<=31
   XZO=INT(XORDER*(25/100))
   XY =XORDER+XZO
   ENDIF 
   IF XD>=1 .AND. XD<=3
   XZO=INT(XORDER*(25/100))
   XY =XORDER+XZO
   ENDI
   XORDER=XY
   ENDI
   
*
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XBULAN.VALUE='TOTAL'
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XHARI.Value=XLAMA
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.CONtainer1.Xjual.Value=TRANSFORM(XTJUAL,"@Z999,999")
   Thisform.pageframe1.page1.CONtainer1.XBELI.Value=TRANSFORM(XTBELI,"@Z999,999")
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.CONtainer1.XRBELI.Value=TRANSFORM(XTRBELI,"@Z999,999")
*
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XRTJUALHR.Value=XPERHARI
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XTERSEDIA.Value=XTERSEDIA
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XBMG.Value=XORDER
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XMG.Value=XMG
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.grid1.SetFocus
ENDPROC

Name = "xmaxbln"
PROCEDURE InteractiveChange
XL=(THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XMAXBLN.Value-1)
XMAX=DATE()-(XL*30)
xtglAWL=(xMAX-DAY(xMAX)+1)
XHARI=DATE()-XTGLAWL
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XACUAN1.Value=XTGLAWL
XACU=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XACUAN1.Value
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.CONtainer1.XHARI.Value=XHARI
*ldTglHariIni = DATE()
*ldAkhirBulan = GOMONTH(ldTglHariIni - DAY(ldTglHariIni) + 1, 1) - 1
*lnJmlHari = DAY(ldAkhirBulan)
ENDPROC

XGOEND
Form1.Pageframe1.Page1
Top = 26
Left = 216
Height = 25
Width = 22
FontBold = .T.

Picture = wzend.bmp
Caption = ""
Enabled = .F.

Name = "XGOEND"
xPROCEDURE Click
XDEP=ALLTRIM(THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XDEP.VALUE)
XKD=ALLTRIM(THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XKODE.Value)
*XCR=XDEP+XKD
XCR=XDEP
XL2=LEN(XKD)
XLL=ZL_DEP
*MESSAGEBOX(XLL)
*MESSAGEBOX(ZLONG_CODE)
IF EMPTY(XDEP)
   MESSAGEBOX("Departemen harus diisi !!",0,"Perhatian !!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xdEP.SetFocus
   RETURN
ENDI   
XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT DISTINCT KODE_BRG FROM BARANG WHERE LEFT(KODE_BRG,?XLL)=?XCR AND LENGTH(TRIM(KODE_BRG))=?ZLONG_CODE ORDER BY KODE_BRG DESC ","BBX")
IF XH<>1
   MESSAGEBOX("File barang gagal dibuka !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page1.xdEP.SetFocus
   retu
ENDI
SELECT BBX
GO TOP
*BROWSE
IF EMPTY(KODE_BRG) 
   *MESSAGEBOX("LEWAT 1")
   XKDNYA=PADL(1,ZPJ_KODE,"0")
ELSE      
   XL2=LEN(ALLTRIM(KODE_BRG))
   XL_NDX=(XL2-ZPJ_KODE)
   IF XL_NDX>ZPJ_KODE .AND. !EMPTY(XKD)
      *MESSAGEBOX(XL_NDX)
      *MESSAGEBOX(ZPJ_KODE)
      *MESSAGEBOX(XKD)
      XUU="1"          
      XKDNYA=XKD+PADL(XUU,ZPJ_KODE-XL_NDX,"0")   
     * MESSAGEBOX("LEWAT 2")   
   ELSE
      XKK=SUBSTR(BBX.KODE_BRG,ZL_DEP+1,ZPJ_KODE)      
      XNO=ALLTRIM(STR(VAL(ALLTRIM(XKK))+1))  
     * MESSAGEBOX(XNO)
      XKDNYA=PADL(XNO,ZPJ_KODE,"0")    
      *MESSAGEBOX("LEWAT 3")     
   ENDIF    
ENDI   
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XKODE.Value=XKDNYA
USE IN BBx
THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page1.XKODE.SetFocus
 
ENDPROC
x

WPROCEDURE InteractiveChange
xpj=LEN(alltrim(thisform.pageframe1.page1.container4.text1.value))
ll=ALLTRIM(thisform.pageframe1.page1.container4.text1.value)
XH=sqlexec(xDS,"SELECT * FROM grup WHERE LEFT(keterangan,?xpj)=?ll order by KETERANGAN","CARIGRUP")

   RETURN
ENDI

simpan
Form1.Pageframe1.Page3
Top = 573
Left = 191
Height = 51
Width = 88
FontBold = .T.
FontSize = 11
Picture = wzsave.bmp
Caption = "\<Simpan"
TabIndex = 104
Name = "simpan"
PROCEDURE Click
    IF THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XJumlah.Value=0
     MESSAGEBOX("Jumlah tidak boleh kosong !!",0,"Perhatian !!")
     thisform.pageframe1.page3.xjumlah.SetFocus
     retu
    ENDI
    xkode_PAKET=thisform.pageframe1.page3.Xkode_paket.Value
    xkode_brg  =thisform.pageframe1.page3.Xkode_Brg.Value
    xacc=thisform.pageframe1.page3.xACC.Value
    xsatuan=thisform.pageframe1.page3.xsatuan.Value
Xhrg_beli=thisform.pageframe1.page3.xhrg_beli.Value
Xhrg_jual=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.Xhrg_jual.Value
XJUMLAH=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XJUmlah.VALUE
XISI=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XISI.Value
XTJUAL=0
xOPR=XUSER
XDATEOPR=DTOC(DATE())+"-"+TIME()
IF EMPTY(XKODE_BRG) .OR. XJUMLAH=0
   MESSAGEBOX("Kode barang dan jumlah tidak boleh kosong !!",0,"PESAN !!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page3.xkode_Brg.SetFocus
   retu
ENDI
IF !xubah
   xh=SQLEXEC(xds,"insert into PAKET (ACC,KODE_PAKET,KODE_BRG,SATUAN,HRG_BELI,HRG_JUAL,JUMLAH,OPR,DATEOPR,ISI) values (?XACC,?XKODE_PAKET,?XKODE_BRG,?XSATUAN,?XHRG_BELI,?XHRG_JUAL,?XJUMLAH,?XOPR,?XDATEOPR,?XISI)")
   IF xh<>1
   
 
   
      MESSAGEBOX("Data PAKET gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
  
      RETU     
   endi   
   
else      
     SELECT PAKET    
     XURUT=PAKET.URUTAN
     x1= "Update PAKET set ACC=?XACC,KODE_BRG=?XKODE_BRG,HRG_BELI=?XHRG_BELI,HRG_JUAL=?XHRG_JUAL,JUMLAH=?XJUMLAH,OPR=?XOPR,DATEOPR=?XDATEOPR where URUTAN=?xURUT"
      
     xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1)
     IF xh<>1
   
 
   
        MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
  
        retu     
     endi  
ENDIF
   XKD=LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page3.XKOde_paket.Value,10)
   xAC=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XACC.Value
   x1="SELECT DISTINCT paket.KODE_BRG,BARANG.NAMA_BRG,paket.HRG_BELI,paket.HRG_JUAL,paket.SATUAN,paket.JUMLAH,paket.ISI,paket.OPR,paket.DATEOPR,paket.FSAT,PAKET.URUTAN "
   x2="FROM paket LEFT JOIN barang ON paket.KODE_BRG = BARANG.KODE_BRG AND PAKET.ACC=BARANG.ACC WHERE PAKET.KODE_PAKET=?XKD AND PAKET.ACC=?XAC "
   x3="ORDER BY PAKET.KODE_PAKET"
   xH=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+x2+x3,"PAKET")
   IF xh<>1 
    MESSAGEBOX("Database paket gagal diakses !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
    RETURN
   ENDI 
   SELECT PAKET
   SUM HRG_JUAL*JUMLAH TO XJUAL
   GO TOP
   SUM HRG_BELI*JUMLAH TO XBELI
   GO TOP
   *BROWSE
   *RETU
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.ZTBELI.Value=XBELI
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.ZTJUAL.VALUE=XJUAL
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"UPDATE BARANG SET HARGA11=?XJUAL WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKODE_PAKET AND ACC=?xACC ")
   IF XH<>1
   MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
  
   retu 
   ENDIF 
   thisform.browse_KOMPOSISI
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE3.grid1.FontBold= .T.
   IF !xubah
  
   *thisform.kosong_barcode
     
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE3.tambah.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE3.ubah.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE3.simpan.Enabled=.t.
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE3.hapus.Enabled=.f.
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE3.batal.Enabled=.t.
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XKode_Brg.Value=" "
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XNAMA_BRG.Value=" "
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XSATUAN.Value=" "
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XHRG_BELI.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XHRG_JUAL.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XJumlah.Value=0
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XISI.Value=0
   thisform.PAGEFRAME1.PAGE3.XKOde_Brg.SetFocus
ELSE
  thisform.browse_KOMPOSISI
ENDIF
xubah=.f.
ENDPROC

hapus
Form1.Pageframe1.Page3
Top = 573
Left = 279
Height = 51
Width = 88
FontBold = .T.
FontSize = 11
Picture = wzdelete.bmp
Caption = "\<Hapus"
TabIndex = 105
Name = "hapus"
HPROCEDURE Click
thisform.pageframe1.page3.tambah.Enabled=.f.
thisform.pageframe1.page3.simpan.Enabled=.f.
thisform.pageframe1.page3.batal.Enabled=.t.
thisform.pageframe1.page3.hapus.Enabled=.f.
thisform.pageframe1.page3.ubah.Enabled=.f.
xKODE_brg=thisform.pageframe1.page3.Xkode_Brg.Value
XKD=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.Xkode_paket.Value
XACC=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XACC.Value
IF EMPTY(XKODE_bRG+XKD)
   MESSAGEBOX("Tidak ada data yang dihapus!!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page3.tambah.SetFocus
   RETURN 
endi
if messagebox("Yakin ' "+Xkode_brg+"' akan dihapus..?",4+32,"Perhatian")=6
   SELECT PAKET 
   XURUTAN=PAKET.URUTAN
   XH=sqlexec(xds,"delete from PAKET where URUTAN=?XURUTAN")
   IF xh<>1 
      MESSAGEBOX("Data Gagal dihapus !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
      RETURN
   ENDI 
   SELECT PAKET
   USE
   x1="SELECT DISTINCT paket.KODE_BRG,BARANG.NAMA_BRG,paket.HRG_BELI,paket.HRG_JUAL,paket.SATUAN,paket.JUMLAH,PAKET.ISI,paket.OPR,paket.DATEOPR,paket.FSAT,PAKET.URUTAN "
   x2="FROM paket LEFT JOIN barang ON paket.KODE_BRG = BARANG.KODE_BRG AND PAKET.ACC=BARANG.ACC WHERE PAKET.KODE_PAKET=?XKD AND PAKET.ACC=?XACC "
   x3="ORDER BY PAKET.KODE_PAKET"
   xH=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1+x2+x3,"PAKET") 
   IF xh<>1 
     MESSAGEBOX("Database PAKET gagal diakses !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
     RETURN
   ENDI 
   SELECT PAKET
   SUM HRG_JUAL*JUMLAH TO XJUAL
   GO TOP
   SUM HRG_BELI*JUMLAH TO XBELI
   GO TOP
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.ZTBELI.Value=XBELI
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.ZTJUAL.VALUE=XJUAL
   SELECT PAKET
   SUM HRG_JUAL*JUMLAH TO XJUAL
   GO TOP
   SUM HRG_BELI*JUMLAH TO XBELI
   GO TOP
   *BROWSE
   *RETU
   XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"UPDATE BARANG SET HARGA11=?XJUAL WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKD AND ACC=?xACC ")
   IF XH<>1
   MESSAGEBOX("Data barcode gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
  
   retu 
   ELSE
      MESSAGEBOX("Data barang akan berubah jika di REFRESH !!",0,"Perhatian !!")
      retu
   
   ENDIF 
   thisform.BROWse_KOMPOSISI
ENDI   
thisform.isi_KOMPOSISI
thisform.TOMbolKOMPOSISI_normal
thisform.pageframe1.page3.Tambah.setfocus
ENDPROC

>PROCEDURE GotFocus
IF !XUBAH
    Xkd=LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page3.xKODE_PAKET.Value,10)
    Xac=LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page3.xACC.Value,2)
    XKODE=" "
    sqlexec(xds,"select KODE_BRG from FBARANG where BARCODE=?xKD order by KODE_BRG","CARI")
SELECT CARI
iF CARI.kode_bRG=" "
   use
   MESSAGEBOX("Kode barang tersebut belum ada didata barcode !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page3.xkode_paket.SetFocus
   RETURN
ELSE
   XKODE=CARI.KODE_BRG
   sqlexec(xds,"select KODE_BRG,PAKET from BARANG where KODE_bRG=?xKODE AND ACC=?XAC and paket=1 order by KODE_BRG","CARI")
   SELECT CARI
   IF CARI.kode_bRG=" "
      use
      MESSAGEBOX("Kode belum ada dimaster barang atau bukan barang komposisi !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
      thisform.pageframe1.page3.xkode_paket.SetFocus
   else 
      THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.xkode_PAKET.Value=cari.kode_brg
  
      use
      thisform.pageframe1.page3.XKOde_Brg.setfocus
   endi    
   
ENDIF
ELSE
  
   thisform.pageframe1.page3.xkode_brg.SetFocus
ENDIF    
      
   
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE GotFocus
IF !XUBAH
    XkODE=LEFT(thisform.pageframe1.page3.xKODE_BRG.Value,10)
    XACC=thisform.pageframe1.page1.xACC.Value
    XH=sqlexec(xds,"select KODE_BRG,NAMA_BRG,HPP_AKHIR,HARGA11,SATUAN1,ISI1 from BARANG where KODE_bRG=?xKODE and acc=?xacc order by KODE_BRG","CARI")
   SELECT CARI
   GO TOP
   IF EMPTY(CARI.kode_bRG)
      use
      MESSAGEBOX("Kode belum ada dimaster barang  !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!!")
      thisform.pageframe1.page3.xkode_BRG.SetFocus
   else 
      THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XNAMA_BRG.Value=CARI.NAMA_bRG
      
      THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.xkode_BRG.Value=cari.kode_brg
 
      THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XSATUAN.Value=cari.satuan1
      THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XHRG_BELI.Value=CARI.HPP_AKHIR
      THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XHRG_JUAL.Value=CARI.HARGA11
      THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page3.XISI.Value=CARI.ISI1
      use
      thisform.pageframe1.page3.XJUMLAH.setfocus
   endi   
ELSE
   thisform.pageframe1.page3.xJUMLAH.SetFocus
ENDIF    
ENDPROC

   x3="ORDER BY PAKET.KODE_PAKET"

     MESSAGEBOX("Database PAKET gagal diakses !!",0,"PERHATIAN !!")
     RETURN
   ENDI

   GO TOP

Form1.Pageframe1.Page4

Name = "simpan"
PROCEDURE Click
    xfgambar=ALLTRIM(thisform.pageframe1.page4.xGAMBAR.Value)
    IF LEN(xfgambar)>25
        MESSAGEBOX("Maaf nama file max 25 character !!",0,"PESAN !!")
        thisform.pageframe1.page4.siMPAN.SetFocus  
        retu 
    endi
   
    XK=brg.kode_brg         
    x1="UPDATE barang SET fgambar=?xFGAMBAR WHERE KODE_BRG=?XK"
xh=SQLEXEC(XDS,X1)
   
IF xh<>1
   MESSAGEBOX("Data gambar gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
       
   thisform.pageframe1.page4.SIMPAN.Enabled=.f.
   RETURN
ELSE
   MESSAGEBOX("Gambar sudah tersimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")
    
   thisform.pageframe1.page4.simPAN.SetFocus
   retu
ENDIF
    
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE Click
xfile=GETFile()
lcString = xfile
lcSeparator = "\"
FOR lnI = 1 TO GETWORDCOUNT(lcString, lcSeparator)
  lcWord = ALLTRIM(GETWORDNUM(lcString, lnI, lcSeparator))       
NEXT
thisform.pageframe1.page4.image1.Picture=xfile
thisform.pageframe1.page4.xgAMBAR.Visible=.f.
thisform.pageframe1.page4.xGAMBAR.Value=lcWord
thisform.pageframe1.page4.image1.Stretch= 2
thisform.pageframe1.page4.simpan.SetFocus
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE InteractiveChange

   ELSE
  XREAL=0
   ENDIF    
ELSE   
   XREAL=0
ENDI     
thisform.pageframe1.page5.xPH11.Value=XREAL 
ENDPROC

textbox
xIsi1
Form1.Pageframe1.Page5
{FontBold = .T.
Height = 25
InputMask = "999,999.999"
Left = 200
TabIndex = 163
Top = 263
Width = 71
Name = "xIsi1"
PPROCEDURE InteractiveChange
*SATUAN 1
xreal=0
XHPP=BRG.HPP_AKHIR
XISI=thisform.pageframe1.page5.xisi1.Value
XHPP=(XHPP*XISI)
XHARGA11=thisform.pageframe1.page5.xharga11.Value
IF XHPP>0 .AND. XHARGA11>0
   IF XHARGA11>0
  xreal=((Xharga11/XHPP)*100)-100
   ELSE
  XREAL=0
   ENDIF    
ELSE   
   XREAL=0
ENDI     
thisform.pageframe1.page5.xPH11.Value=XREAL 
XHARGA12=thisform.pageframe1.page5.xharga12.Value

XTUNAI=1
XJT_TEMPO=XTGL_ORDER+XTERMIN
IF XPPN=1
   XJFPPN=1
ELSE
   XJFPPN=4
ENDI   
USE
IF EMPTY(XSATUAN)
   MESSAGEBOX("Satuan harus diisi !!",0,"PESAN !!")  
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XSATUAN.SetFocus
   RETU
ENDIF 
IF xjumlah<=0
   MESSAGEBOX("Jumlah harus diisi !!",0,"PESAN !!")  
   THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.Xjumlah.SetFocus
   RETU
ENDIF 
XH=SQLEXEC(xDS,"SELECT KODE_BRG FROM "+XFL+" WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKODE_BRG ","YY")
SELECT YY
GO TOP
IF !EMPTY(ALLTRIM(KODE_BRG))
   *MESSAGEBOX("Barang tersebut sudah Ada !!",0,"Perhatian !!")
   thisform.pageframe1.page6.XJumlah.SetFocus
   XTMB=.F.
ENDIF
SELECT BRG 
IF XTMB
    XQ1="Insert Into "+XFL+" (BARCODE,KODE_BRG,NAMA_BRG,SATUAN,JUMLAH,HRG_BELI,DISC1,DISC2,DISC3,DISC_RP,ISI,CODESUP,NAMA_SUP,ALAMAT_SUP,TGL_ORDER,LAMA,JFPPN,JT_TEMPO,TUNAI,GRUP,KET,BONUS,D1,D2,D3,D4) values "
    XQ2=" (?XBARCODE,?XKODE_BRG,?XNAMA_BRG,?XSATUAN,?XJUMLAH,?XHRG_BELI,?XDISC1,?XDISC2,?XDISC3,?XDISC_RP,?XISI,?XCODESUP,?XNAMA_SUP,?XALAMAT_SUP,?XTGL_ORDER,?XTERMIN,?XJFPPN,?XJT_TEMPO,?XTUNAI,?XGRUP,?XKET,?XBONUS,?XD1,?XD2,?XD3,?XD4) "
    xh=SQLEXEC(xds,XQ1+XQ2)
 ELSE
    XQ1="UPDATE "+XFL+" SET SATUAN=?XSATUAN,JUMLAH=?XJUMLAH,HRG_BELI=?XHRG_BELI,DISC1=?xDISC1,DISC2=?xDISC2,DISC3=?xDISC3,DISC_RP=?XDISC_RP,ISI=?xISI,CODESUP=?xCODESUP,NAMA_SUP=?XNAMA_SUP,ALAMAT_SUP=?XALAMAT_SUP,"
    XQ2="TGL_ORDER=?XTGL_ORDER,LAMA=?XTERMIN,JFPPN=?XJFPPN,JT_TEMPO=?xJT_TEMPO,TUNAI=?xTUNAI,GRUP=?XGRUP,KET=?XKET,BONUS=?XBONUS,D1=?XD1,D2=?XD2,D3=?xD3,D4=?xD4 WHERE BARCODE=?XBARCODE"
    xh=SQLEXEC(xds,XQ1+XQ2)
 ENDI   
 IF xh<>1
  MESSAGEBOX("Data ORDER Gagal disimpan !!",0,"PESAN !!")  
  THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.SIMPAN.SetFocus
 endi  
 xh=SQLEXEC(xds,"UPDATE "+XFL+" SET CODESUP=?XCODESUP,NAMA_SUP=?XNAMA_SUP,ALAMAT_SUP=?XALAMAT_SUP,TGL_ORDER=?xTGL_ORDER")
 IF xh<>1
  MESSAGEBOX("Data ORDER Gagal diupdate !!",0,"PESAN !!")  
  THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.SIMPAN.SetFocus
 endi  
 thisform.pageframe1.page1.SetFocus
thisform.Pageframe1.Page1.Grid1.SetFocus 
ENDPROC

 XSAT=ALLTRIM(THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XSATUAN.Value)
 XKD=THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XKOde_Brg.Value
IF thisform.pageframe1.page6.XBONUS.Value=1 
  XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT KODE_BRG,BARCODE FROM FBARANG WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKD AND SATUAN=?XSAT AND SP=1","TT")
  SELECT TT 
  GO TOP
  IF EMPTY(BARCODE)
     MESSAGEBOX("Barcode Bonus belum terdaftar !!",0,"Perhatian !!")
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XBONUS.SetFocus
     USE IN TT
     RETU
  ELSE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XBarcode.Value=TT.BARCODE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XHRG_BELI.Value=0
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XKet.Value="BONUS "    
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XJUMLAH.Value=0   
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XJumlah.SetFocus
     XTMB=.T.
     USE IN TT 
     RETU     
  ENDI   
ELSE
  XH=SQLEXEC(XDS,"SELECT KODE_BRG,BARCODE FROM FBARANG WHERE KODE_BRG=?XKD AND SATUAN=?XSAT AND SP=0","TT")
  SELECT TT 
  GO TOP
  XTMP=.F.
  IF EMPTY(BARCODE)
     MESSAGEBOX("Barcode Bonus belum terdaftar !!",0,"Perhatian !!")
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XBONUS.SetFocus
     USE IN TT
     RETU
  ELSE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XBarcode.Value=TT.BARCODE
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XHRG_BELI.Value=XHRG_ORDER
      THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XKet.Value=" "    
     THISFORM.Pageframe1.Page6.XJumlah.SetFocus
     USE IN TT 
     XTMB=.F.
     RETU     
  ENDI 
ENDI
ENDPROC
